2017-12-28 20:14:51
Madhura Mukherjee
239753
4.0
I've visited City Centre branch of Haka before, but this was my first visit to the Mani square one. I've had my Chinese a la carte at Haka, but this the first time I sampled their buffet. Firstly, the place is nicely done and has a good vibe about it. The buffet was reasonably priced, with a minor surcharge if one wishes to have prawn, since that is not included in the buffet. The Haka chicken soup was just the right amount of tangy, to set your taste buds dancing on a wintry afternoon. For starters, there were prawn wafers, chicken drumsticks, chicken Waltons, veg wantons and spicy potato. Starters were pretty good, especially the chicken drumsticks(Hong Kong style) and the spicy potato. Main course comprised of the usual fare : egg fried rice, chicken hakka noodles, a chicken and fish gravy preparation each. It was nothing fancy, just good old conventional Chinese. Special mention should be made of butter garlic veg noodles.For dessert, there were pastry, brownie, darsan and ice cream. I quite liked the buffet and would look forward to visit again. I just wish they could add a complimentary soft drink to the buffet, that would make it oh-so-good :).

##

2017-12-27 04:07:34
Akash
29069086
4.5
Haka is one of the popular destination for all chinese cuisine lovers in town and being a hardcore this place was in my wishlist for a long time. Finally today I got a chance to visit this restaurant to fulfill my chinese food craving. So let's come and explore this place.

Location & Ambiance - Haka situated on the 4th floor of the Mani Square Mall. The place usually remain crowded throughout the lunch and dinner time. I visit this restaurant around 1:30PM today and it was pretty much filled up with crowd and luckily got a table for myself without sanding in queue. The Place is really big in size with continuous music at background. Stuffs are really helpful, courteous, highly professional and always ready to take care about their customers' satisfaction.

Menu - Now come to the food part. I choose to have Non Veg Buffet which includes One non Veg Soup, 2 types of Non-veg starter item as well as 2 types of veg starter also, 2 types of main courses, 2 types of side dishes and desserts.

Soup - In Soup section, thay had Chicken Clear Corn soup. The Soup was good in taste but had little lack of salt into it. just add some salt & pepper and you are ready to go.

Starter - In starter section they had Vegetable fried wonton and Crispy vegetable konjeenaro as veg starter and Chicken Siu mai and Drums of Heaven (Hong Kong Style) as a non-veg starter.
Fried Wonton was too crispy from outside but I feel less filling inside of it. Crispy vegetable konjeenaro was excellent. With crispy texture from outside and soft from inside, the item is must try item here. Now come to the non veg starter section, Chicken Siu mai very good. Moist outer coating with chicken filling at centre the dish is heavenly for any Dimsum lovers. If the above mentioned items were good, then Drums of Heaven was really the showstopper. Crispy fried chicken with perfectly mixed sauce, the item tastes like heavenly.

Main Course - In the main section they had Sichuan Chicken Noodles as well as Chicken Fried rice. The noodle was good but hardly had any veggies in it. With soft touch of sauce, the noodle tastes good. Now come to the fried rice section, well cooked rice was carefully cooked with lots of chicken and eggs. Both the main items were good but was oily in nature, especially the fried rice.

Side Dish - In the side dish section they had Hot and Garlic Chicken and Fish in chilli mustard sauce. The chicken had no extraordinary touch, just like traditional Hot & Garlic chicken. But on the other hand the fish was just mind-blowing. Thin layered Basa fish was cooked in mustard sauce. Taste-wise it was quite different but I like it.

Desserts - In desserts section they had Darsaan, Cake, Desserts of the day, Mousse & 4 types of ice cream i.e Vanilla, Orange, Chocolate, Tutti Frutti. Darsaan was warm in nature, cake was good but the desserts of the day was pretty hard. Ice Cream was good as usual and the mousse was just perfect.

After telling my lunch experience, I especially want to mention the name of Mr. Prasant, Restaurant Manager of HAKA in my review for showing much courtesy. His polite behaviour, warm greetings really made my dining experience a grand one. Overall it was a great dining experiences from my side and definitely visit this restaurant again.

I was a regular at this place during my school days. A good buffet after a odd movie, or a birthday celebration haka was the place for us. Always a big fan of Speciality Restaurant and their brand of food haka became a regular hang out for us heavy eaters. The decor is nothing fancy but quite nice and easy on the eye. Well to begin with the starters drums of heaven, or dimsums or fried wantons loaded with chicken and good to tatse. The soup is okayish with again a good amount of meat. The main course is not very fancy like the rice and chowmein over my numerous visits have not been something awesome but good at that price. What amazes me is that be it chicken prawn or fish in the main course there will be one dish which manages to stand out. I love their mustard fish or schezwan fish. Their chili chicken is also good. As the buffet menu changes over time so it is kind of difficult to keep track. But overall with newer options like crab and lamb in weekends they have kept their foothold. Now coming to the dessert section, the part which many heavy buffet eaters target is quite good at their price. I have had ice cream of 4different flavours in haka along with accompaniments like chocolate sauce, chips etc darsaan, cakes and mousse. The drinking option is there so you can easily go for something you like. Mainly this place gives you a buffet spread at a much pocket friendly rate and is total value for money. The staff is quite courteous and during weekends and holidays they get quite a rush So that gives you an idea how good they are. But lastly their a LA carte food quality js much better in taste though prices are higher.

2017-11-28 01:45:22
Anuvab Biswas

4.0
If you're on a tight budget but still crave for a Chinese buffet,visit Haka at the Mani Square Mall. I've visited this place on multiple occasions and hence I've forgotten the exact menus on those specific days.

For starters,two items that stood out were-the Chicken Wantons and the Drums of Heaven.
Combine the crispness of the wantons and the juiciness of the drumsticks(more like lollipops)and you'd like to eat that forever and not proceed for main course.
Other items in starters include clear soup,crispy chilli potatoe and dimsums(or suimai).

In the main course I had concentrated less on the fried rice/chowmein,and more on the chicken and fish preparations.
The rice and chowmein were average.
The side dishes keep changing and I think they include crab,prawns and lamb on weekends(not sure).

Moving on to dessert, choose your flavour of ice cream from 5 different flavours.
Then there's darsaan,cakes,pastries and pudding,all of which were good.

Like after any other buffet,I initially had difficulty in moving as I'd stuffed myself up too much(starters mainly). 
The dining experience was good. Service was good and refilling of food counters were prompt.
They also have offers on drinks and certain dishes from the √† la carte menu.

2017-10-27 18:22:03
Shreya Chakraborty/tinkering_tastebuds

4.0
I have always loved the simple Chinese food that the Speciality Restaurants churn out. I have previously been to the other outlet of Haka at City Centre 1 and loved it, so when I had to choose a place to dine in with my cousins at Mani Square, Haka wasn't a tough choice. The unlimited buffet priced at 499 AI definitely helped in making that decision!

The buffet isn't grand, like the ones you would expect in some places. However, the food is delicious and the price is definitely way less than most places. Starting from the soup to the barbequed potato and chicken wings to the beautiful fish preparation for the main course and ultimately, the blueberry mousse and mango ice cream - almost all the dishes will satiate your stomach. The staffs are courteous and friendly. Overall, a happy atmosphere for happy dining!

2017-10-24 15:50:06
Sayantika Sen
36135596
4.0
We went there during Kali Puja Morning. We went for the Chinese buffet. That day the buffet price was Rs 560 but on regular weekdays the price will be Rs 480. We went there between 12:30-3.

Food :

Starter :
Chicken Soup
Pan fried fish (specially available on 560 buffet)
Chicken drumsticks
chicken wantons

Main Course:
Fried rice
noodles
Mustard chicken
prawn curry (available on 480 buffet with additional Rs69)
another fish item (I don't remember the name)

Salad:
papad
fried noodles
cucumber soaked in vinegar
achari salad

Dessert:
Pudding Sandesh
Blueberry moose
ice cream (vanilla, chocolate, strawberry, mango)
darsan
(with unlimited choco sauce, choco chips, jelly and nutty topping)

I suggest you to visit the place for the dessert and starter (pan fried fish and chicken drumsticks). The main course was okayish.

Staff:
The restaurant staff were polite and well mannered. They were personally taking care of us and settled every issue.

Interior:
The restaurant is well decorated, specially the wall papers attracted my view. Overall it was a nice experience.

We decided to have buffet today. So an economical option was haka. The waiting time was nearly half an hour. The starters were ok except that the fish was loaded with cornflour so I could hardly taste the fish. The chilli baby corn were amazing as were the chicken suimai. Main course had Singapore chilli crab and prawn and chicken which were quite good. Now coming to the desserts, I did expect Haka to come with a fruit platter atleast but sadly they did not have it. Also there was only one varient of mousse. Now coming to the ice cream quality, it tasted grainy which means the milk quality used wasn't too good. You could specially feel the graininess in vanilla (which by the way, is my all time favourite). So overall I have given it a 3.5 experience. Haka please improve slightly further more.

Located on the top floor of Mani Square this is a must visit place for all the buffet lovers!

Decor: Brightly painted walls and fairly comfortable seating arrangements. Nothing to brag about.

Staff: Polite and listens to you. Has fair knowledge of what they are serving.

Food: This steals the show without a doubt. We always try their buffet. The soups are amazing coupled with lip smacking chicken lollipops. Starters are good and so are the mains. They put out separately cooked dishes for vegetarians, a very good gesture. They have improved the dessert section and it is fairly strong. The best thing is unlimited soft drinks at a very nominal price.

Overall: Great food at a stellar price. A must visit specially for college and school goers.
A shout out to the manager who interacts with each customer to cater to their needs.

2017-10-01 17:49:36
Dwaipayan Chakraborty
35453470
4.0
Ambience: Located at the top floor of Mani Square beside Machaan and Hoppipola, this place is a Chinese lover's ideal place. Spacious with buffet service, this restaurant offers complete satisfaction for the hungry one. The walls are filled with graffiti and the tables are arranged in fours and eights primarily. Place is well maintained and pretty standard.

Food: Since it specializes mostly on chinese cuisine, the buffets items contain chinese items mainly. The Soups and the starters are tasty and fill the stomach in a better way than the main course ones. The main course noodles and side dishes (mostly chicken and fish) are bland and does not serve the required purpose of palate satisfaction. Again the desserts come as a welcome surprise with ample variation in taste and flavor. 

Service : Service is okayish. Nothing great but nothing to criticise either. Cash and card both accepted. And the waiters oblige to clicking your group photos willingly. :)

2017-09-06 00:05:35
Pradarshita Ray
42159777
4.5
If you are craving for plateful of Chinese cuisine then visiting Haka for a buffet lunch at Mani Square would be something really blissful. And if you can make it out on one of the weekdays, the experience would turn out to be really profitable as it just costs Rs. 440.
Coming to the menu, one would served with a bowl of hot soup (either Veg or Non-veg) followed by starters - Dumplings, Chicken Drumsticks, Crispy vegetables and two other veg starts which I didn't taste. The soup was really good - hot, thick and was filled with grated vegetables, paneer and chicken, you may add the pan fried noodles to it and have it like chop suey. The stuffings in the Dumplings had a unique taste, one would find it hard to have enough of it and the crispy vegetables were tasty too. The main course had two options both for rice and noodles, the Ginger fried rice had a nice taste. Apart from that there was Garlic Chicken and Fish. However, their was no option for prawns. One can have them on extra payment. The desserts were yummy too, it had Daarsaan, Mousse, bread pudding and ice-creams of various flavours with hot chocolate syrup, choco chips etc.
Perhaps had a great time there and would recommend it for food lovers. Just a reminder, do not take excessive food on your plate and then waste it. :-)

There was two types of noodles and two varieties of rice. There were two side dishes of chicken. All of them were good. Coming to the desserts, they had darsaan, banana mousse which was delicious, strawberry tarts and four varieties of ice cream with four different toppings. The strawberry one was a turn down. 4.5
I have tried haka at city centre before but this is the first time that I visited the mani square outlet. My parents had celebrated their anniversary here with their close friends . The spread was value for money . There were chicken lollipops, stir fried prawns , stir fried cauliflower , spicy potato sticks , veg and non-veg wantons and hot and sour soup both veg and non-veg for starters . We had ordered fresh lime, beer and iced tea separately as well . In the main course there were 2 varieties of fried rice and noodles each ;veg and non veg . There was a chicken side dish , a fish side dish and 2 veg side dishes , one comprising of a tasty mix of vegetables. The desserts comprised 4 varieties of ice-cream with chocate sauce , nuts , chocate chips and crispy cruchies as toppings , a mango mousse and a pineapple fruit cake . I didn't particularly like their fruit cake. Other than that everything else was nice , especially the starters. This is one of the best budget buffets in town and they serve good quality food regardless of the day you go. Will definitely visit them again.

2017-07-21 13:40:43
Amarnath Biswas
32959335
4.0
Situated at the well known mall of Mani square, this restaurant is situated at the top floor of the building. The restaurant serves only Chinese cuisine. We went for lunch. It was little bit surprising to me as the manager said that they only have the option of buffet and there is no option of Ala carte menu. Left with no option we had to go for buffet, but it was worth it to me. There was a wide option of menu laid out for non veg as well as veg people. The starters were served on the table and were refilled as soon as our platters were empty. The flavors were real good and fresh. The main course was available with option of rice or noodles, with gravy option of chicken and prawn. The Datsun in the dessert and the mousse just took away my breath. All in all i enjoyed the food thoroughly. 

One striking thing to me was the ambiance, it not at all went with the theme of the restaurant. The ceiling especially looked horrible as if no efforts were put to make that look better. Although the staffs were very courteous and helpful, but i guess the dining experience could have been better in a better ambiance. 

For people who love Chinese cuisine, MUST try here for once.

LOCATION--Located on the top floor of mani square is quite a nice place. Their buffet meal is @‚Çπ575. We have visited haka on a sunday for their lunch buffet.  

STARTERS--Coming to the food they have served us three non veg starters which were meat balls, drums of heaven and chilli crab. The meat balls were very tasty and the crab tasted nice. The drums of heaven wasn't good enough. They also had few other veg starters which were not tried. 

MAINS--Moving to the maincourse, the section was starter+new items. So it was a repeat of the exact items tried moments back plus some few more. The newer items in the non veg section had fish in mustad sauce, shrimps, and a dish made out of chicken and chashewnuts. They also had fried rice and noodles. The veg section too had some additions. They also two variants in the soup section, salads, sauces, and papads. 


DESSERTS--The dessert section did fill our hearts. They had mini cupcakes, mousse(vanilla and strawberry), another sweet dish, four variants of ice cream(vanilla,mango,strawberry and chocolate) and the toppings section had hot chocolate sauce, choco chips, crushed butterscotch and jello.

It was a nice buffet meal at this budget. Overall a nice place to visit and offers a friendly environment. Refer to my account for pictures.

¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The ambience is good and so is the service. 2017-06-28 23:56:42
Upasana
6567551
3.5
One of my friend gave his birthday treat at haka, mani square. It was lovely experiencing a buffet only @575 still they need to improve on their main course.
The starters consisted of drums of heaven, crab, momo, fried wanton, and a chicken sweet corn soup.
All tasted good except the momo which we all felt that it only consisted of cabbage leaves and nothing else. Though it was written chicken sweet corn soup but it contained very little amount of chicken.
Now coming to the main course there was chicken hakka noodled which was okayish in taste and egg fried rice which was blunt in taste. Apart from that there was chicken, fish and prawn which were average in taste and nothing special. 
But the dessert won our heart. There was mousse, darsan, four flavours of ice cream and mango pastry... everything were very nice to eat.
So the main thing is that starters and desserts were the only best things in the buffet. The staffs were courteous and helpful.

Haka is a great place if one is looking for an affordable Chinese buffet with fairly delicious food. Their buffet comprising of one soup, a couple of veg and non veg starters, salads, noodles, fried rice, a fish dish, a chicken dish (in the non veg section) and assorted desserts is value for money. All the dishes including the desserts tasted good. Loved the chicken drumsticks and veg sui mai. However I wish they had included a couple of dishes in the main course and starters, but then again it costs around ‚Çπ500 per head. There is also an offer of paying ‚Çπ65 extra for a 8pcs prawn dish in a sauce of your choice.  The unlimited soft drinks offer is valid only for lunch.

Haka has been around for quite sometime now and it shows on the furniture which looked worse for wear somewhat. However the ambience is good, great for a family outing or meal with friends. The service is satisfactory. Overall, it's a good place for affordable and tasty Chinese food.

##

2017-06-13 22:08:04
Debaleena
31102218
4.5
Went there yesterday with my brother and his girlfriend to celebrate my brother's birthday. We opted for the non veg lunch buffet along with one plate of prawn in hunan sauce for the added price of Rs. 69 + tax and unlimited refills of pepsi for Rs. 39 + tax. A good deal indeed.
About the food, to clarify at first, I am not a great connoisseur of fine dining experiences so the review is based on that basis. Infact this was my first buffet and I found it good enough to meet my expectations. I have heard that the variety in Haka is less compared to other buffets in the city however I think, so is the price, so one cannot really complain. The starters are served at the table remaining items are self serviced. We were first served a chicken soup (sweet corn chicken soup if I remember correctly). Soup was good enough, I am a soup person so maybe expected it to be a lttle thicker but what was served was definitely not bad. There were two types of chicken starters and the prawn was served as a starter which we had as an add on to the buffet. I loved the prawn dish. The prawn was succulent and soft and cooked with perfection blending with the hunan sauce. The chicken items were good but nothing special. I found the main course better than the starters. The chow mein was quiet tasty and the fried rice was good enough. There were prawn crackers too. The sides included a chicken and a fish item. I liked the fish item better but the chicken was nice too. Coming to the deserts. There was darsan which I didn't have, a mousse which was super yummy and not too sweet, a bread pudding which was great and four flavours of ice cream with choice of toppings.

The service was really good, the manager visited our table a few times to ask if we were enjoying our meal. The waiting staff were efficient and polite and removed the used plates and cutlery from the tables as soon as the course was done. The cold drinks refill is a good option coz they keep filling up your glass throughout the meal without having to call them to refill.

We went on a monday afternoon and the place was brimming with people. And was kind of noisy but I guess you can't blame the restaurant for that. There was a huge led television that was broadcasting cricket so sports enthusiasts might like that.

Overall a definite thumbs up from me and hope to visit again.

Its a cheap chinese buffet, and thats about it.
The place is nice,well lit and spacious. But they had a tv which was playing cricket and that kind of spoils the mood. 
The service was not upto the mark at all. My family and I went there this monday for lunch and the guy who was supposed to give us a table kept us waiting for 10 mins even though the place was nearly empty.
They also take really long to restock the food.
Now for  starters they had chicken soup, wafers, chopsuey, drums of heaven, kimchi and wanton. The soup was nice and tasty. But the wanton was a let down. It was cold,soft and soggy. Personally among the starters the drums of heaven was my fav. The spices were well balanced and the chicken was soft and tender.
I was disappointed to find no crabs or prawn on the menu even though I heard they serve crab legs. Guess thats only on weekends.
Now in the main course were egg noodles,chicken fried rice,chili chicken and schezwan fish.
Both the noodles and rice were good. Both had loads of egg or chicken and cooked with little oil.
But the chili chicken was dull,had no taste and for some reason was loaded with black pepper. The fish on the other hand was too salty. The main was a big letdown
For desert they served darshan,mousse,chocolate cake and 4 flavours of oce cream. The darshan was nice but the star of the entire lunch was the mousse.
It was freaking amazing. The ice cream was ordinary.

However who complains when you get to eat a sumptous meal in just 450 bucks along with unlimited Pepsi.

The place which I frequent the most in Kolkata due to a cheap buffet at a price of just 432/-

At this price, you get a non veg/veg soup, prawn crackers, chicken drumsticks (which are rather floury but... well... who's complaining), chicken wontons/sui mais, two veg starters, chicken fried rice and noodles with their vegetarian counterparts and three gravy items in non-vegetarian - Chicken fish and prawn. Weekends also have a crab starter with these.
There are also  a trio of vegetarian gravy dishes.

For desserts, there is chocolate mousse, two types of cakes, brownies, as well as four different types of icecream with three types of toppings for them.

The cheap price and a moderately passable taste makes this the best option if you want to fill your stomach without making your pockets empty.

##

2017-04-26 20:51:50
Chandrani Sadhukhan
5554601
4.0
Had yesterday off so we decided to try this budget buffet place. 
We arrived at 1 pm and opted for non-veg buffet.
They serve the soup and starters, main course is self-serving. 

You can add unlimited soft drinks at Only 39/- so better go for it because in other places they charge around 90 bucks for the same. 

Starters : 
1. non-veg soup, don't remember the name (2.5/5) maybe because I'm not really a fan of it. When asking if they have any other kind of soup the waiter said he would ask the chef, but I wasn't much interested in soup so I let it go. 

2. Chicken dimsums (4.5/5) they were they best starter item so we got two more plates. Wanted another plate but decided against it in favor of making space for main course, regretted it later.

3. Fried wontons (2/5) least favorite

4. Drums of heaven (3.5/5) didn't order more of it in favor of dumplings. 

Main course : 

1. Egg fried rice (2.5/5) not good not bad 
2. Noodles (3/5) okayish but better than fried rice 
3. Hot garlic chicken (3.5/5) 
4. Fish item wasn't good either. (3/5)

That's it. Basically their main course isn't their "main" focus. Its always the starter and desserts that steal the show. 

Desserts: 
Apart from vanilla, chocolate and mango ice creams the chocolate mousse cake was the best (4.5/5). I didn't try the darsan. Mango cheese cake was okay (3.5/5) 

Honestly, despite their main course being a big let down, their starters and desserts are bang for buck and I didn't feel that much disappointed. Those dimsums are still calling me back. 

Ambience : 3.5/5 
Seating : 4/5 
Food : 3.5/5 
Staff : 4/5 
Pocket pinch was 1000 bucks for two and totally  justified.

2017-02-15 09:50:00

1322109
4.5
Located at the topmost floor just opposite to Chapter 2 at Mani Square Mall. The decor and ambience on the occasion of Valentine's Day turned to be gorgeous and we were lucky to get a seat as soon as we entered. We went for the special buffet menu for lunch. We were served with Chicken Sweetcorn Soup at our table and the service turned out to be amazing. Really, the staff deserves to be applauded. Coming to the food, the buffet menu was enormous and we had a huge journey from the starters to the desserts. The veg items along with the non-veg ones were delicious just as the other. The starters are something which will make you want for more and more especially the Chicken Lollipop , the tasty Dimsums and the Fried Crabs. Food quality is absolutely top knotch. The main course left us dumbstruck as we were in a dilemma to choose among the many delicacies. Chicken Noodles, Chicken Rice along with One Fish, One Shrimp and One Chicken Side dish was great and left us craving for more. Coming to the desserts, Ice cream( Mango/Strawberry/Chocolate/Vanilla), Darsan, Mousse Cake along with Chocochips, Chocolate sauce and another Sauce (green) turned to be excellent. Fresh Lime Soda which we ordered were good too. Price is absolutely pocket-friendly. The Manager is friendly and courteous. Everything seemed to be on point. On occasion of Valentine's Day, we also received two chocolates from them too.

I assure that one would not be disappointed with Haka for sure. Recommended.

So for me the food (that evening) was not great but the service and ambience was good. So the points are mostly for the service.

Well, I am writing this review after my 17th visit to this place.
When you want Chinese with a touch of the Speciality Group(which also owns Mainland China,Sigree,Asia Kitchen,Machaan,Caf√© Mezzuna) and low on budget too, this should be your ultimate stop. This place has a new neighbour in Mani Square, Chapter 2  (course spread lacks variety and is not tempting.)
Except Haka no one can serve better Chinese buffet at a price of around 500 rupees(inclusive taxes). Haka has a new competitor in City Center 1 area(Since 2016),which is doing pretty well; but it is impossible to match Haka's standard and variety.
Haka has a well trained team working both in the kitchen and in the dining area. The manager is extremely courteous and the impressive part is the manager works in tandem with the entire team in serving or paying heed to any customer's demand and also keeps a check on the feedbacks provided by the guests.
When it's Chinese,it's Mainland China.
But, when you want to go easy on the pocket, it's Haka.

Haka at City Centre (Saltlake) is better than its twin in Mani Square.

P.S. you get a complimentary mocktail if you are a ICICI Bank card holder and unlimited soft drinks at a minimal price.

2016-09-08 09:50:07
Gaurav Sarkar
6784031
3.5
HAKA is a famous Chinese joint located inside the ManiSquare mall near Kankurgachi. They serve only buffet here and there is no option of a-la cart√©.
We were a group of 7 hungry boys who decided to celebrate the occasion of getting placed for our first job.
The lunch buffet starts here at 12.45 pm. It was a weekday and the price for weekday lunch buffet is rs 431 all inclusive. There were two add on options available with the buffet.. for rs 59+tax u could get 8 pcs of prawns and for rs 35+tax, u cud avail unlimited soft drinks of ur choice.
We chose the lunch buffet and the unlimited soft drinks option and our bill amounted to 477 per head inclusive of all.
The decor is preety good. It is spacious and resembles a high quality restuarant , although a bit more renovation and good arrangement of seats with bright lightning will  really gv this place a lift.
Coming to the food..
Starters:
1. Chicken surmai: it was lyk chicken dumplings. Tasted average. Nothing to brag about. It lacked flavor but had a pungent smell of minced chicken. Was moist. Not really a very tasty dish.
2. Chicken Drums of Heaven: crisp fried chicken tossed in a very delectable sauce. It was fantastic and tasted very good. Best dish offered..certainly their usp.
3.Chicken soup: average.with really tiny bits of chicken which seem negligible.
Starter and soup served on the table by servers and the repeats came quickly enough.
Main course :
Preety boring. Could not have much. The fried rice and the chowmein were preety average and bland. They had egg noodles and egg chicken fried rice as staple. There were fried veg wantons, chilli french fries, stir fried veggies, cottage cheese in veg while for nonveg they kept just a fish and a chicken dish. The fish was good and the chicken preety average.
The main dishes lacked variety and it was a disappointment!!
The desserts were limited but the darsan was really good. Mousse was okayish. Standard ice creams with hot chocolate sauce. Limited but good.
For the price, many ll say that they justify the buffet items. However mains need a little more variety and flavors. With so many buffet joints popping up every now and den, haka will face stiff competition.
USP is low cost and drums of heaven.
Typical indianized chinese is served. Dont xpct much.. average affair.. service was decent!!

At Rs 431/- per person ( including tax ) it is value for money but some more variety in buffet is always welcome even if it comes a bit costlier.

POCKET PINCH : Reasonable and at 543/- inclusive of taxes it is one of the more budget options. Thus, the price is the only stand point with a trade off that is variety and choices.

2016-06-22 17:15:58
Adhiraj Sarker
257292
3.5
Haka, the name strikes a chord with those looking for a Chinese buffet spread at a reasonable price. Hence it's a big hit with students like me.  But one will be surprised to see people of all ages availing their buffet. Who after all wants to miss a decent Chinese buffet at such a good  price?

I've been to this outlet of Haka for a couple of times. Being reasonably priced it has its own pros and cons.  What I like is the politeness of the staff, the unlimited cold drink for Rs. 35, lip smacking chicken drumsticks. The service is so good that the containers are refilled even before they're empty. The cons include bland maincourse items, and less variety of everything.

The Chicken Manchow Soup tastes quite delicious. Having the Chicken Drumsticks and Crispy Chilli Potato alongwith is a blissful affair. The Chicken Siumai doesn't taste appealing. As you enter the maincourse section you're in for a little disappointment. The Chicken Fried Rice and Noodles taste bland. The Chilli Chicken is a careless preparation. The Basa Fish in a light sauce tastes good. Desserts section has 4 different flavours of ice creams, and a too sweet mousse!  

Buffet spread in Haka is a mix of good and bad. If one overlooks the few hitches they're gong to have a wonderful experience. Paying by ICICI card entitles you to a free mocktail. However I feel quality is not the same as before, even after raising the buffet price to Rs 431 for a Friday lunch.

2016-05-20 08:29:10
Poumita Das
2810584
3.5
Went there for a Sunday buffet lunch. Absolute value for money restro. Albeit the items provided are nothing out of the ordinary yet the price is unbelievably low. Probably the lowest price available for a Chinese buffet lunch in Kolkata.

The non veg starters were tasty - Chicken fried wontons and Shandong chicken drums(recommended) however the chicken manchow soup was fabulous (it's my favorite so I might b a bit biased to it). The veg starters included veg suimai( not recommended) and crispy vegetables which I did not taste cz it didn't look appealing. There was one vegetable soup as well which again I gave a miss. The salads were poor. Neither pickled cucumber nor Kim chi tasted fresh. The main course consisted of a number of options. There was Corn n potatoes in tsing hoi sauce which was okayish. Next was vegetables in Chilly Basil sauce which was an absolute disaster. Then comes chicken Hakka noodles and chicken fried rice both of which tasted very nice. Chicken in Sichuan sauce tasted more of a soup than a side dish as the gravy was toot thin and tasted bland. Same for the Shrimp dish. The star of the show was fish in parsley sauce. Not very spicy yet tasty. Dessert section was undoubtedly the best.Darsaan ( again my fav) with four different flavor of ice creams n chocolate sauce, mousse and cakes. Special mention of the mousse which was absolutely wizard. The cakes were nice too. By the end of the meal I was too full n could hardly move. This place is obviously not one of the must visits however recommended for college students for the dirt cheap prices.

2016-04-17 00:25:20
Pramit Mitra
31146427
4.0
Had this in my sights since my Mio Amore visit on Christmas day last year; finally made it today on the 163rd birthday of Indian Railways...
On 16th April, 1853, the first ever train rolled in India from Mumbai to Thane. Whilst, on 16th April, 2016, two bosom friends from school and I rolled out in this sweltering heat for Mani Square.
Once at Haka, we were treated graciously and given a confirmation seat. Being Saturday, it was quite full. We opted for the weekend Non Veg Buffet meal. 
They served us the soup, Chicken Coriander Soup, and the starters, Chicken Fried Wonton and Drums of Heaven Hong Kong Style. While the drums could have been better, the fried chicken couldn't have been any better! Sticks to my tongue even now as I sit to pen down my experience.
A friend and I also ordered 30 ml of Johnnie Walker black label each to add some alcoholic touch to our meal.
In the main course, they offered Chicken Hakka Noodles and Chicken Fried Rice. Being out and out non-vegetarians, we concentrated only on the non-veg section. The Hakka noodles was the best I've had in the recent times but was seriously disappointed with the fried rice. They can look at improving it's taste a bit more.
Accompanying the above were Chicken in Hot Garlic Sauce, Fish in Chili Mustard Sauce and Prawn in Chili Basil Sauce. I personally don't have Prawn but loved the other two to the hilt, specially the fish was out of the world.
To complement things, they also served some fine dessert which included Hiraan, strawberry cream, Mousse cake and assorted ice creams; vanilla, chocolate, strawberry and mango favoured.
Overall a fine place to dine if your mind speaks Chinese anytime. The fact they offer drinks is also a plus factor. The staff are very courteous and well behaved. To top it all, the ambient atmosphere keeps you at ease always...go for it!!!

##

2016-04-09 20:08:01
Debashish Dey - Petukbangali.com
424506
4.0
After planning for decades about going for a buffet lunch at haka, i finally managed it . I went there early because it was weekend and I had a movie to catch at 2pm . I later realized it was a pretty good decision since the place gets really crowded after 1 15 pm Saturday weekend .

The very disciplined waiters greeted us and after taking our orders they served the starters . We skipped the soups . For starters the non veg items are : - 

1. Chicken siumai ( 3.5 / 5 ) - These are crispy fried chicken wantons . They were served with a mustard sauce . They tasted good . We didnot ask for a refill but the items were quite good for a one timer .

2. Drums of heaven hunan style ( 4 / 5 ) - This is the star of this buffet place . It is not an uncommon dish . You may get the saucy chicken drums in any Chinese outlet but here you can much on them as much as you like and fulfill your drumstick desires . We had 2 plates of them

After these we took a mini 5 minute break and went ahead with the main course :-

1. Chicken fried Rice ( 3 / 5 ) - Quite an average fried rice . Was looking forward to it since i am a serious fried rice eater but it was not cooked to utter perfection .

2. Coriender rice noodles ( 3.5 / 5 ) - This was better than the rice . Was skeptical at first but they got the flavor right here .

3. Fish in mustard sauce ( 4 / 5 ) - This is a value of money dish . The dish was a bit salty but it connected . This fish was " makhmali " to say the least . You can have a lot of pieces and you can still carry on .

4 . prawn hunan style  ( 3 / 5 ) - Now this dish is only available in the weekend . But inspite of having huge expectations with this dish , it didnot leave much of a mark . Had a lot of chilli flakes in it which put us off . The prawn pieces had a lot of arrowroot coating so definitely could not have a lot of it .

As for the veg items in the main course , there are really not much to offer . 2 veg curries which tasted pretty ordinary and the noodles and fried rice was not much of a mood enhancer too .So a strictly no no for the veggies .

Then we took another 5 minute break to our stomach and went on with the deserts . There were pastries but we were eager to jump on the darshaan and assorted ice cream which needs no ratings .

All in all it was a good one timer with the drums of heaven and fish in the main course as the best of the lot. There are soups, salads for you to try so I belive for 370 rupees this should be a good one time experience if you are in Mani square and have the appetite for a small buffet lunch .

The staff is very very courteous and helpful . The sweet lime soda was cool and the manager kept of asking about the quality of food which I felt sincere . So those who have not yet tried the place can have a go for atleast once .

Location : 4th level, Mani Square.

‚ÄúChinese lovers‚Ä¶eat all you can‚Äù

The place is spacious and the ambience has a chilled out feel to it. The vibes are subtle to sooth you while you dine at one of the leading Chinese cuisine restaurants in the city. The d√©cor pretty much suits the ambience and is plain and simple. Unpretentious and comfortable furniture too. The main and only attraction is their excellent buffet menu which is so reasonably priced despite variety of dishes to quench your thirst for authentic chinese. And there is no option of a la carte so we had to go for buffet.

The food we had was some real deal, although not at par with the other category leaders, but gives a tough competiton.
‚òÖ¬†¬† ¬†Honey Potato : I would say I have had better, but these weren‚Äôt bad either. Pure taste honey with potato tickles your taste buds but the coating was a bit chewy.

‚òÖ¬†¬† ¬†Crispy Chilli Babycorn : A signature Chinese starter and it was prepared the that way. All areas checked out fine. Just a little snag was that the spice element was not up to the mark.

‚òÖ¬†¬† ¬†Vegetable Fried Wontons : These tasted satisfactory. The coating was thin and crisp on the outer areas. However they were undercooked on the inner side which dampened the taste.

‚òÖ¬†¬† ¬†Fried Rice & Paneer in Manchurian Sauce : The fried rice was nice with evenly cut vegetables. The Manchurian sauce was awesome with great spice elements.

‚òÖ¬†¬† ¬†Darsaan & Bread and Butter Pudding Mousse : Darsaan is a classic and can never taste bad, so eventually it was great. The pudding mousse, however, was on a totally different level altogether. And combine it with chocolate sauce‚Ä¶what a wonder. It was so smooth and soft that it would melt in the mouth just as soon as it went in. An absolute peach.

Despite the food had some minor flaws it is not devoid of quality. And offering such a wide variety at such a low price is a rarity. The service too was a delight. The staffs are courteous and manage tables well while keeping a constant tab on the needs of their customers.

2016-03-16 01:02:04
Farhan Ahmad
29640700
4.5
Excellent is one word to describe this place. My experience started yesterday at lunch(tuesday) and at the end of it I just had best wishes for this place.
We were three ppl, 2 vegetarians along with me(pure nonveg). To begin with we were very warmly welcomed by the manager and seated at any place of our liking as half the place was empty. Its spacious and the shade of red in there decor goes well with the ambiance.
Only buffet here. My veggie friends were quite sceptical about it before coming here as most of the reviews have been from the nonveg ppl. I could guess that very few vegetarians visit here from the fact that they were very happy to serve my friends and assured them that most of the dishes they would be served will be prepared fresh for them and took the pain of asking how the preparation was, most of the time. Not so for me though but I didn't have any issues with that as the nonveg food had many takers and was being replenished time to time by hot food.
Coming to the food,it started of with lemon pepper clear soup. A gud light way to cleanse ur palate before ur meal. My starters comprised of chicken drumstick and chicken wantons. Both of them were lipsmacking and I had two servings of each. My friends were served chilli babycorn, veg stir fry and green dimsums. The baby corn was too good. The best I have had till date. Stir fry gud. Dim sum though different but average in taste. Not to forget all veg items freshly prepared and piping hot. My main course had mixed noodles, meat fried rice, chicken chilli like dish and honey chilli fish. All except the fish were ordinary. The fish was heavenly, too gud. I cud see almost everyone eating there rooting for it. The veggies again had a dish extra(read freshly prepared). Chilli veggies, potato corn mix, and a paneer dish(the best amongst them), veg rice and chilli garlic noodles. The impression was mixed on the main course as it was not as good as the starters, a few things though did stand out.
Finally, for deserts there was darsan and ice cream(4 flavours) and mousse. The mousse was very delicious. All creamy, with a slight taste of coffee along with shaved chocolate in it. The ice cream was as usual with hot chocolate sauce and darsan at ur disposal. A debit card offer thanks to my friend, got us a round of free kiwi based mocktail which was very refreshing.
Paying ‚Çπ390(incl. of taxes) per person at the end of the meal, I felt very satisfied with the experience. I feel the lack in variety is justified. Not to forget the excellent service and treatment by the staff who readily accepted every feedback. The team is doing a great job led ably by their manager.
A suggestion though from our side would be to take more care of the main course. There is a lot of scope for improvement there. Also a complimentary drink should be added along with the buffet, (although u can have unlimited cold drinks by just adding ‚Çπ35)

##

2015-12-26 09:19:24
Oishik Sarkar
3119605
3.0
It was a private party from one of my friend & the Shack was booked for it. All the foods were provided by Haka over in Shacks place.

Location : Shack is located just beside Haka on the top or 4th floor of Mani Square Mall.

Decorations : Haka is having a great place inside for handling lots of people while serving them buffets. Sitting are comfortable & ambience is quite good.

Staffs & Management : Staffs of Haka were decently behaved. Manager is very caring to their customers. But one thing seemed odd to me was their sizes of plates were very small & the size of spoon & fork was very big compared to the plates. It was quite hard to handle those big forks & spoons on that small plate. You may feel falling the spoons & forks while filling up your plate, it made me quite uncomfortable while having the foods too.

Buffets : Haka is places into the Great Buffet collections of Zomato & their Buffet stays almost same with the following items...

Salad : Salad of the buffet were nicely decorated with 5-6 items. Salads were average but pickles were not so good.

Starters...
Drums of Shangdong Style : Soft, nicely fried chicken lollypop tossed into dark spicy sauces just touched my heart from very first bite & increased the expectations of the buffet from Haka. This chicken pieces tasted really good to me but a pinch of salt would have been great.

Cottage Cheese In Sichuan Chilli Sauce :  Diced Paneer Pieces were crispy fried outside & tossed into dark spicy Sichuan chilli sauce. Lots of spices felt in the mouth but as per name I was expecting good cheese fragrance from it, unfortunately it was not there. Diced capsicum & onion pieces increased its richness, but same as the chicken dish it was little less on salt.

Pan Fried Crispy Chilli Fish : Big fish pieces covered with crispy fried layer outside & it was juicy inside. Natural taste of fish felt well in mouth & quite tasty.

Mains....
Corn, Potato Tsing Hot Style : I don't know who would love potato & corn in their Buffet. Well somehow it was the first mains of buffet. Although it was cooked well & balance spices were there still it didn't tasted good in my mouth.

Stir Fried Vegetables : Mixed colly flower, carrot, cabbage, capsicum etc were dipped into white sauce. All the vegetables were not well cooked & some felt hard on mouth too. Gravy & the dish itself was washed out spices & didn't tasted good.

Vegetable Hakka Noodles : The noodles were very thick but soft, very less vegetables were used, spices & oil were minimum. Noodles itself tasted not good but combining with side dishes it felt quite good to eat.

Chicken Fried Rice : The rice grains were of average quality. Chicken pieces were hard to find & vegetables too. Very less oily & very less spicy. It tasted below average & very lite. Same as noodles side dish tasted good with it.
 
Fish In Fresh Chilli Coriander Sauce : Big, soft, over cooked fish pieces were dipped into white sauces with diced vegetables. Fish pieces were so soft from outside to inside that it was melting in the mouth that this kind of dishes didn't meant to be. Also the fish pieces has lost its taste due to overcooking & gravy was almost tasteless even with other dishes.

General Tao's Chicken : Big nicely cooked soft juicy chicken pieces were dipped into rich looking gravy. This dish tasted really good with noodles & rice both. It looked very rich & spicy but in mouth it was an excellent combination of spices & chillies. Capsicums & onions took the taste of gravy, while chicken felt the same from inside too.

Shrimps in Spicy Chilli Sauce : It was an item of prawn. Small prawns were dipped into rich looking gravy with capsicums, onions & red chillies in it. It was cooked really well & tasted very nice with rice & noodles.

Desserts....
Daarsaan : Crispy fried chips tossed into dark sweet sauce with lite spices & small beans for fragrance, it was such an awesome desert after dinner. It was something that is dedicated for all sweet lovers & as a sweet lover I liked its taste too.

Chocolate Brownies : With lots of nuts & chocolate chips each & every piece of the brownies tasted great & felt soft in the mouth. Brownies were very small on size but I just loved it's taste, so I took 10-12 of it.

Vanilla Ice Cream : The Ice Cream they served were on the average side. Don't expect BR's quality from a budget buffet but it felt nice in filled up tummy. You can even add chocolate sauce on it for extra flavour.

Pricing : Usually Haka's buffet costs Rs. 376-471 depends upon on offers & timing. This is known as the most affordable buffet in town & it definitely holds that tag. Even for Rs. 25 unlimited cold drinks adds another charm to it. In my scenario the buffet was a part of the party & total package costs near about Rs. 90k for hiring the Shack from 5-11pm on Sunday.

Conclusion : A must visit for every buffet lovers. But don't go with too much expectations, you will only get the quality you are paying for. In some scenario foods are really good, in some average but overall very good buffet specially when you are more focused on starters & deserts.

##

2015-12-24 19:36:31
Sanhita Ganguly
32183676
4.5
This place has been on my wishlist for a long time. I have heard my friends rave about it and the curiosity to see if Haka lives up to the hype, was getting unbearable! :P

The Haka outlet at Mani Square, E.M. Bypass, located on the floor above the food court, is subtly done up in tones of red and black, with soft lighting, good music and helpful staff.

The afternoon lunch buffet had an amazing spread. We opted to add ‚Çπ35 to our bill(without taxes) for unlimited Pepsi. There were 2 choices of soup, and 2 choices of veg and non veg starters each. We went for the chicken suimai(basically, mini momos) and the chicken drumsticks. The soup was delicious, hot and tangy, just the way I like it. The quality of the starters came as a surprise for me. Although I have been to plenty restaurants and tasted the same food, these momos and drumsticks were prepared to perfection. The chicken was soft, tasty and with just the right hint of flavour. We couldn't help taking second servings of both the items. The pickled cucumber for salad, had a weird taste and gets a thumbs down from me.

The main course was a disappointment. The hakka noodles were rubbery and frankly, inedible for me. The fish in lemon and honey sauce didn't do wonders for my taste buds either. However, the shrimp was good. Unable to have the noodles, I opted for the egg fried rice and chilli chicken and both were satisfactory. I would request the management to bring in more choices for the main course. The egg fried rice and rubbery noodles do not make for a good meal. 

Anyway, after the disappointing main course, the desserts took our heart away. Though we were too full to have anything else, the mousse with chocolate sauce was so heavenly that we couldn't stop going back for more. Not having much of a sweet tooth myself, I'd still say that my Haka experience was worth it only for their mousse(and starters, too). Their were four choices of ice cream. The chocolate ice cream was amazing. And so was the Darsaan. 
I did not opt for any vegetarian dish. So can't review that! 

Coming to the service, I found the staff humble, courteous and efficient. The pepsi that we had paid for, kept appearing like magic, everytime, the moment we put down the empty glass, without even having to ask for it. Very rarely have I seen the staff so helpful and polite as I did at Haka.

To sum up, I'd give Haka a thumbs up and urge you to go. Though the main course leaves a lot to be desired, Haka makes up for it through the amazing staff, starters and dessert. Also, the pocket pinch is possibly the least in town.

5) Butter fried noodles
6) Chicken something ( Tastes like plain chilli chicken...good thing unlike earlier now its boneless)
7)Fish in sauce
8) Darsaan
9) Mousse (cream)
10) Chocolate sauce
11) 4 types of ice cream to choose from.

Pocket friendly but quality is going down.
OK now for price sensitive customers like me, this is how they calculate:-
1) Base Price ( found in zomato, usually written like "Amt+TAX")
2) Service Charge@ Rs. 29.5 ( a new component dint see that before and also unsure whether its per person/table, etc)
3) VAT @ 14.5% on (Base Price +Serv. Charge)
4) Service Tax @ 5.6 % on (Base Price+Serv. Charge)
5) Swatch Bharat Cess @0.2% on (Base Price+Serv. Charge)
6) Total ( All inclusive):- 1+2+3+4+5

Therefore a weekday lunch @295+Tax comes to Rs. 390 (All Inclusive).
¬†Now its 450/- AI on weekdays lunch..Prices as on 26/05/2017.

My earlier review:-I have been to this place before, Excellent Chinese Buffet at pocket friendly prices however must mention that some of the items especially from their veg & soup section have degraded...However their non-veg section still manages to steal my heart at so pocket friendly prices.

##

2015-11-18 04:07:36
Sayantani Mandal
5491371
5.0
Words aren't enough to describe the love I have for Haka. It has been my go-to restaurant over the years and at one point, I literally used to go here every day. 
Not only are they the most reasonably priced buffet place in town but the Chinese they serve is even better than Mainland China's, in my opinion, just that they have less variety. The prawn preparation they have in their weekend buffet, the Drums of Heaven among the starters and the Brownies among the desserts are super duper delicious. Basically, all the dishes in their buffet spread are. 
I've literally lost count of the number of times I've been here but they have not failed to please me even once. Though they are the most crowded restaurant in Mani Square, the servers are attentive towards each and every single customer. This place has the most well behaved staff members and managers. One time, in the suggestion sheet I had suggested that they should have brownies in their buffet every day, and to my utter surprise and delight, there they were with a plateful of complimentary hot brownies covered with chocolate sauce, they had from earlier their lunch buffet menu! That was the sweetest gesture ever. 
Also, the interior done up in hues of red and black does great things to your appetite and the ambience is nice too. You can also add unlimited servings of soft drinks to your lunch buffet for just ‚Çπ25. 

Haka rocks! I'm never going to get over this place.

I usually visit haka very less as it is so far away from my place. But today me and my fiance were in the mood for some chinese and we decided to try haka. I had been to the city centre haka once but it is my first visit to the mani sq. outlet. Located on the 4th floor this is a gem of a place. It wont say it is a big restaurant but it has got ample amount of sitting arrangements. 

The staffs were very polite. Now the food- first we took the soup. The veg one was tomato and the nonveg one was a soy based chicken soup, tangy and refreshing.
In the buffet menu there were wantons and chili chickn drumsticks and with the usual noodles,rice and one fish and chicken item. Over to veg there was a manchurian and dumplings and noodle and rice as usual. Now the food tasted good no doubt.. But i want to point out and say that the chicken and fish in the menu tasted almost same,both with a soy gravy..i mean the fish could have been made like some other preparation.

Off the menu they served us a paneer prep which was really really yum..the darsaan was fun. There were brownies and icecream with choclate sauce in desserts..

We had two breezers which cost us an extra 360 with added tax..other than that the price was reasonable..
Definitely worth going if you have not been already.

Haka is owned by speciality group. I went there on a weekday dinner. I entered the restaurant as early as 7 pm. I was well greeted and shown my table. At INR 414 AI , its were cheaply priced for a buffet. Though being a pure vegeterian I always feel that items offered to us in buffets are always less in compsrison to non veg people but they compensated us by offering one extra starter & main course each. Decor was average. Staffs were well trained and they keep on asking if I like the food.
Coming to food items. Lemon corriander soup was divine. Just loved it. In starters, fried wonton & vegetable salt & pepper were served hot and it tasted amazing. Crispy chili babycorn, the extra starter, was average. The starters & souos were served on table. But I was suprised to find these starters in buffet also. When I tasted the same starters from buffet, It was not hot & that tasty. Have conveyed the same to the management.
Main course offered were ordinary. Hakka noodles, fried rice , veg potato corn in chili soya sauce & stir fried vegetable with dry red chili. Firstly all the items in buffet were not hot. So it effected the taste. But when I conveyed the same to the staff they immediately prepared fresh and hot for me. That was nice of them.
Deserts were good. Specially I liked mousse and chocolate icecream with chocolate sauce. 
Overall the experience was decent but buffet food need to be improved and should be served hot.

One of my worst dining experiences ever - this place really sucks !
Casually, went to Mani Square as it was a Sunday evening. Just strolling around, learnt that Haka @ 5th floor is offering buffets at Rs. 214 (A.I.) from 4 pm - 6 pm. Had heard decent reviews about this place earlier, so, decided to give a try.
Entered the restaurant at around 4:30 pm and noticed that the tables were still being cleaned and more than half the items to be served were not ready, so, waited for around 20 minutes. Since buffet was discounted, only a few items were offered - which is perfectly ok.
Ambience appeared decent as the seating arrangements were designed to appear China-like. Also, an LCD was playing a Cricket match.

For Veg starters, only Veg Salt and Pepper was there, which was cold and downmarket. It contained only half-fried potatoes - I barely had 2-3 pcs of the same. For main course, Veg Fried Rice was there which was decent and Veg Noodles - which I did not taste. Corn Potato Chilli gravy was also there, but surprisingly,¬†the staff told that no bowls are available for serving this gravy. Ultimately, I had to carry the gravy in a quarter plate. I have seen better standards in road side dhabas ! For salad, cucumber along with a couple of carrot slices and kimchi was there.
As soon as I went for the second helping, a staff came and hurriedly cleaned my table - I do not know why! Is this the hotel etiquettes taught to Haka staff?

As per the menu, Chocolate ice cream was to be served, but they served vanilla ice cream. I requested for correcting this, which was done in sometime.

Darsaan was available, which was crisp and nice.
The staff was very rude - as if he were doing a favour allowing me to eat. Somebody told that buffet gets over at 5:30 pm, somebody told at 5:45 and somebody told that it gets over at 6 pm - they just wanted the customers to gulp down some food and leave. Service is very poor. I am very sure that a couple of staff were bitching about me for reasons, which I do not know - perhaps, may be because I was casually dressed or may be I had multiple servings of desserts. I could make this out as they were looking at me and laughing.
Most indecent behaviour I have ever seen !
I was not having free food - I have paid for whatever I was having, so, I will not take this shit !
I simple paid the bill and walked off without tipping !

Request the management that if they are serving food at discount, they should not atleast discount the service quality, infrastructure and decency.

3.5
We just went to Mani Square for a Movie on last Saturday. It ends near 2 pm. We both feel hungry. We plan to eat KFC Chicken, but we thought why not try HAKA Restaurant. We know that they only serve Shrimp on Weekends. So we change the plan and move to HAKA. At 2.30 pm we found that HAKA totally full house. We put our booking in their guestbook. After 10 mins we found a table. They offer 471/- with all taxes for weekend buffet lunch, also extra 25+7/- for unlimited cold drinks. We took both offer. It is probably the cheapest  but standard Chinese Buffet in Kolkata I think. It's just beyond perfect for pocket friendly yet a grand (almost) dinning with friends, family or colleagues.

We saw the entire restaurant is full and good to see that everyone enjoyed the food. They told us that they only serve the Soup and the 1st plate of Starter. After that you can join the mob who gathers almost every time near the buffet table. 

On the buffet menu they served with Spicy Tomato Basil Soup, Chicken Sweet Corn Soup,  Veg Dimsums, Potato Fry, Chicken Wantons, Chicken Lollipop, Chili Paneer, Veg Noodles, Veg  Fried Rice, Egg Chicken Fried Rice, Egg Chicken Hakka Noodles, Haka Chili Chicken in Sauce, Fish in Green Sauce, Shrimp in Red Sause, Darsaan, 4 type of Ice Cream Flavor Mango, Chocolate, Vanilla & Tutti Frutti with Chocolate Sauce and Pinapple Cake and Wanton type one desert preparation, made with coconut.

The Chicken Sweet Corn Soup was good, Chicken Wantons, Chicken Lollipop was Awesome taste. I took lots of pieces, both. Veg Dimsums, Potato Fry also had good taste. Non Veg Noodles was good, but Non Vrg Rice too simple like normal rice. Chicken item was average taste, Fish item also average taste, but the Basha fish itself very soft and tasty. The Shrimp was good and spicy also. Next move on to desert section where I found only Ice Cream is a good option. Others were very average. Darsaan taste like Khaja. Ice Cream with Chocolate Sauce always my choice. I enjoyed the Ice Cream twice. Here only I ate the main course because their main course items were also good taste. With this budget I am satisfied what they were served. Only I miss one extra starter. I think for that reason I give them 3.5. Haka is too Good, but not like MAINLAND CHINA.Haka's food is delicious, especially Chicken Wonton I found very interesting.

The Ambience is very classy. I like that. The service also good and prompt. For example,  whenever you leave your table, they change the used plates. Overall a nice experience with affordable Chinese Buffet and highly recommended.

2015-06-25 03:30:33
Shaunak Guharay
1301830
4.5
Haka is known for its buffet, especially among the student circle. It is owned by the Specialty Restaurant chain (the same group which owns Mainland China, Flame & Grill and Oh! Calcutta).

Haka is extremely affordable, has quality food, good ambience and really pleasant and helpful staff.

I have been to Haka 3-4 times now, and their food taste is quite consistent, but the buffet items are kinda repetitive.
Nevertheless, the buffet is really good value for money. Food is refilled every few minutes, and is always hot and fresh.
The Vegetarian selection was kinda meager, but the non veg section was really good.
Location of the restaurant is in the top floor of Mani Square, extremely easy to find.

Overall a 4.5/5.0 for me, -0.5 for lack of variety in buffet. A must visit for college goers, big foodies or anyone who would love to have Chinese without breaking the bank.

2015-05-21 16:34:37
Sourajit Karmakar

4.0
Pocket friendly and tasty chinese buffet, variety is less though.

If you want to have a good chinese buffet at affordable prices then this is the place to be. They probably offer the cheapest buffet in kolkata. Seating arrangements are good, ambience average. Waiters are friendly but service may be slow at times. Its better to go through the buffet items yourself and take what you like rather than waiting for the waiters to serve you the starters and all.

The variety of items offered in buffet is small. Two veg starters and two non veg starter. Veg starters are average. But the fried chicken wanton is just awesome. The other chicken starter is good too. They make awesome snacks along with beer. Main course offers noodles, fried rice, garlic chicken, veg manchurian etc. Noodles are tasteless, i would suggest only go for the rice. Garlic chicken is okaish. The desert offers only four flavours of ice creams and chocolet sauce, i guess cant expect much given the price. Overall a good buffet option, nothing extra ordinary.

Update:  After quite a while, recently went for a saturday dinner buffet. Although prices has gone up, i must say the food quality has improved too. This time the chicken drumstick was even better. Main course items had general tao' s chicken, items with fish and shrimps etc. Desert had more options and all were satisfactory. Weekend dinner buffet costs rs 543 all included. Updating my previously given 3.5 rating to 4.

2015-05-01 14:46:06
Anubhov Kanjilal
1445384
3.5
**Location = 4th Floor, Mani Square Mall, EM ByPass.

**Brief = I have been there many a times, mostly after watching movies at CineMax.

**Ambiance = Pretty large and spacious. The seats are comfortable and they give you a warm welcome always.

**Things Tried = My preference have mostly been the buffet, it being one of the cheapest in Kolkata.

In starters they provide Chicken Clear Soup with the Prawn wafers(Papads), the soup tastes okay-ish with chicken chunks.
Then comes the Chicken Fried Wantons and Chicken Drumsticks. The drumsticks are spicy and very soft. The wantons taste decent with the sauce.

One can opt for Unlimited Beverages(soft) by spending Rs.25/- extra.
I obviously try it everytime, ending up drinking 5-6 glasses of them.

In the Main Course, they have Egg fried rice, Chicken hakka Chow,Hunan Chicken and a fish item, which tastes better than all the rest. They dont have much items in the buffet spread, which I feel a bit disappointing.

One can try similar Veg buffet spread also, but after gobbling too much of starters and the main courses, I haven't had the calibre to try them.

In the desserts you have darsan(sweet chips),chocolate rolls,Mousse,Ice creams and hot chocolate sauce.

**Recommended = The non-veg buffet is quite satisfying.

**Service = Always they serve you with a smile, and they duly inquire about your needs.

**Purse Check = Rs.800/- for 2 people on a Weekday (Non Veg Buffet lunch). Very cheap :P

**Overall = A good place to have some decent buffet in cheap prices.

Cheers Haka :P

2015-04-25 11:09:26
Utsav Ganguly
2537814
4.0
Present on the 4th floor of Mani Square, Haka offers arguably one of the cheapest Chinese buffets in Kolkata. I went for a lunch buffet on a Sunday. The sheer choice was staggering. One could pick dishes from both the veg and the non veg sections simultaneously. The soup with the prawn crackers at the start of the meal was quite hearty. This was followed by some Chinese salads, among which the kimchi stood out as a clear winner. Among the starters the one that clearly stood out was the hot basil chicken. The noodles and rice themselves were quite unimpressive in terms of flavour, but the main dishes were quite good. Even the dessert section provided an array of choices, from four different flavours of ice-cream to pastries, brownies and of course, Darsaan, that staple of the indo-chinese restaurant. Is it the very best chinese you can have in town? No, not really. But, considering the price range, it is certainly an offer that cannot be refused.

I have been a fan of Haka since 2011, when I visited this place for the first time. Nothing too fancy, yet a place that serves a nice fare at such cheap prices. I have only tried the buffet and never felt like trying out the a la carte, though i have heard the a la carte to be better. Anyways, i think haka is the cheapest chinese buffet available in kolkata. So whenever im short of cash, but need to satisfy the foodie in me, i head straight to haka.
Coming to the food. Some find it too good. Some, like me, find it okayish, not too bad, not to good. And some hate it. The soup that they serve in the weekday lunch is alright. The weekend dinner soup is heavy and nice. I eat too many prawn chips with it, every single time. Haha! I'M IN LOVE WITH THE KIMCHI. Its tangy, spicy and a mess of heaven. I always eat too much of kimchis in my every visit. Since im not much of a spicy food lover, i cut down the spice content with pickled cucumbers. I love it so much so, that i eat some of it even after dessert to keep the taste in my mouth for long *wink*
Among the starters, the one that everyone takes in abundance is the chicken lollipop thing. Its really crispy, tangy and oh-so-good. I also love the chicken momos that they serve in the weekend dinner. The veg wontons are nice. Everything else is OKAY.
Coming to the main course, i totally heart the prawn item they serve in the weekend dinner. Its the best among the mains i feel. I also like the thai fish from the weekday lunch. The fried rice is forever bland, no matter when you go. So i take the noodles. Its good. The fish in oyster sauce, doesnt taste the same. But palatable. The chicken items are good. Haka doesnt have a huge spread, so theres nothing much to choose from, especially on a weekday lunch.
The dessert always have the darsaan and ice creams. In the weekend dinner they have fruit custard and a bread pudding in addition. I cant eat too much of sweets, so i stick to the ice cream mainly. And the brownie slice from weekday lunch.
Overall haka is averagely satisfactory. I dont mind going there time and again. For lunch, they have an offer of unlimited soft drink at 25rs extra. The price is really reasonable. Recommended. Cheerie!

2015-01-03 00:19:20
Subhasish Das
2646
4.0
Haka is targeted at diners looking for an affordable yet filling Chinese buffet. I did not go with high expectations but I must say that I was pleasantly surprised. Today my colleagues decided to go out for a quick dinner and we landed up at Haka (Mani square). The buffet was priced very reasonably at Rs 475 (All inclusive)¬†

There were 2 soups (1 veg and 1 non veg), 2 Veg and 3 non veg appetizers. A couple of veg main course and 3 non veg main course items along with Fried rice and noodles.¬†

The soup and starters were served on the table along with some prawn chips, pickled cucumbers and some tangy kimchi. The soup tasted nice along with drums of heaven, fried chicken wanton and a Fish (Basa) appetizer. The fish appetizer was not upto the mark and did not have much filling. The wanton was average but the drumsticks were pretty good.¬†
Since there were not much veg options and most of the stuff was almost over, the waiter served us crispy chili baby corn which was indeed very tasty. There was one cauliflower appetizer as well which we liked. We were later served with crispy mixed veg preparation which was also good to taste.¬†

Next up was the main course which consisted of chicken, fish and shrimps. The chicken and shrimp preparation was really impressive. The shrimps were pretty big in size and can be compared to normal prawn sizes. I was very much happy with the main course. The noodles was average and so was the fried rice.¬†

Then came the desserts. There was darsaan, brownie slices, normal custard, caramel custard and 4 flavours of ice cream with chocolate sauce. I simply loved the desserts and could not help stuffing myself to the brim !¬†

Over all it was a great dining experience. I was really not expecting so many options at a budget buffet restaurant and thus I would strongly recommend this buffet if someone is not looking for something very fancy. The staff is polite and goes out of the way to please customers. We were served 2 out of the buffet dishes which is indeed appreciation worthy.¬†

A solid 4 for HAKA :)

2014-11-06 17:35:12
Piko Biswas
410422
4.5
This place is amazing. One of the few places in Kolkata still serving standard buffet at reasonable prices. I've been here loads of times, with family, with friends, with a small group and with a group of 20-something people. They accomodate everyone with a smile. Their buffet menu, especially the weekend menu has an astounding number of items, with each one tasting better than the other. They usually have two soups, a whole lot of starters, salads and prawn crackers to begin with. Their drumsticks in a spicy, garlic-flavoured sauce and tiny steamed chicken dumplings are my absolute favourites. Sometimes I pile my plate high with these tiny dumplings and the delicious accompanying sauce and have gobbling competitions with my cousins. :P They have quite a lot of variety for vegetarians, with a completely separate main course section for them. The non-vegetarian section on weekends, is stuffed to bursting with chicken, prawn, fish all cooked till soft and juicy, in various sauces that are simultaneously light and creamy and smooth and robust. Flavour is never compromised, and their sauces taste great no matter what name it has. The main carbs, i.e. rice and noodles are also light and non-greasy with plenty of vegetables and chicken. The deserts section is overflowing. Darsaan, brownies, petit fours, custard, fruit, chocolate sauce, ice-cream and so much more. It varies each time I've been, but has never failed to excite me.

The food containers are refilled as soon as they empty with hot, amazing food of wonderful quality. Eat all you want. A 4.5 only because my vegetarian friend was a bit disappointed with the vegetarian starters.

(3) Kimchi
(4) Steamed Chicken Momo
(5) Hunan Chicken
(6) Veg Fried Rice
(7) Veg Hakka Chowmein
(8) Egg Fried Rice
(9) Chilly Chciken
(10) Chilly Fish
(11) Ice-Cream (3 different flavours)

The Hunan Chicken was crispy and tasted delicious when savoured with unconventionally concocted tomato chilly sauce. Steamed Chicken Momo along-with Veg Soup helped in replenishing the empty belly right at the start.¬†

The Lemon Soda, sipped in between, shall tickle your gustatory senses to crave for more.
The scoops of 3 different flavors of Ice-Creams, with some chocolate sauce spread over them, towards the end served as the fitting dessert.This one is a self-service place, but the staffs showed promptitude in clearing the discarded plates off the table.¬†
The ambiance was good; the place was brightly illuminated; the paintings on the walls were soothing to the eyes; the 24" television-set added yet another feather to its decor.
Overall, a within-the-budget place to stop by, especially when you are celebrating the birthdays of four of your buddies. :)

2014-07-21 21:03:09
Arpita Sarkar
2883858
3.0
Haka, a moderately priced restaurant in town for Chinese buffet.  Last weekend I went there with my pals for lunch. We had to wait for a while, coz it usually remains crowded. The ambience needs no special mention because it is already well known for its bustling and enchanting decor. So, moving on to the food section. We started with the soups, it had Veg Corn soup and Chicken Hot and Sour soup which was palatable, accompanied with the crispy noodles and prawn wafers. Yes, no doubt, the soup was hot and tasty which added a zing to my mood. Then the starters, consisted of two non veg dishes (which was disappointing, being a non-veg) and a few veg dishes (mustard potato, one more potato dish, dimsums, a dish with baby corn). I didn‚Äôt try any of the potato items, the dimsums were soft filled with corn and the baby corn dish was fine. There was only Chicken Wontons and Chicken Drumsticks in the non-veg section. The wontons were up to the mark, and so were the drumsticks. The wontons had the perfect chicken flavor, served with a spicy sauce. I love that salty taste in drumsticks and they served the perfect one. One round of starters (few of my friends went for some more rounds  :P ) and then we moved on to the main course. The first thing that dismayed my attention was the lack of Chicken dishes in this section. It had  Chicken Hakka Noodles, Mixed Fried Rice ( it should be called egg rice, coz it only had fried  egg pieces, there was no sign of prawn or chicken on it), Hot and Garlic Chicken, Mustard Prawn and one more fish item ( sorry for not remembering the name).  The noodles were mouth watering and also the chicken dish. The gravy of Hot and Garlic chicken was so nicely cooked. The fish preparation was good enough but I just don‚Äôt know what to say about the rice, the taste was bland.  The Mustard Prawn was proper Sorshe Chingri ( our very own Bengali dish), and I don‚Äôt know what the chef tried to make. It was the odd one out!!  After this little disappointment, I was glad to see the desert section. The chocolate mousse (awesome), cakes, three kinds of ice creams(vanilla, chocolate, mango , served with hot chocolate sauce and one orange flavored sauce) and darshan  blew my mood. The chocolate mousse was too good (it was not coated with dark chocolate layer and that was the best part), the fruit cakes were soft and flavorsome. The desert section was simple yet nice. 

I expected a little more and hope to get it by my next visit. They should add some more dishes in the main course, atleast in the weekend menu. For that if they want to charge more then definitely they should go for it!!
